---

## Accessibility Annotations

### General Accessibility Features

1. **Keyboard Navigation**
   - Tab order follows logical reading flow
   - Skip navigation links available
   - Focus indicators clearly visible (2px solid outline)
   - All interactive elements keyboard accessible

2. **Screen Reader Support**
   - ARIA labels for all icons and buttons
   - ARIA live regions for dynamic content
   - Semantic HTML structure (header, nav, main, aside)
   - Alt text for all images and illustrations

3. **Color & Contrast**
   - All text meets WCAG AA contrast ratio (4.5:1 for normal, 3:1 for large)
   - Color never sole indicator (icons, labels, patterns used)
   - High contrast mode support
   - Colorblind-friendly palette

4. **Text & Readability**
   - Minimum font size: 14px (mobile), 16px (desktop)
   - Maximum line length: 80 characters
   - Line height: 1.5 for body text, 1.2 for headings
   - Resizable text up to 200% without loss of functionality

5. **Touch Targets**
   - Minimum size: 44x44px (iOS), 48x48px (Android)
   - Adequate spacing between interactive elements (8px minimum)
   - No reliance on hover states for critical information

6. **Forms**
   - Clear labels for all inputs
   - Error messages associated with fields (aria-describedby)
   - Required fields clearly marked
   - Autocomplete attributes for common fields

---

## Design Notes

### Responsive Breakpoints

- **Mobile**: 320px - 639px (sm)
- **Tablet**: 640px - 1023px (md)
- **Desktop**: 1024px - 1439px (lg)
- **Large Desktop**: 1440px+ (xl)

### Animation Guidelines

- **Micro-interactions**: 200ms ease-in-out
- **Transitions**: 300ms ease
- **Page transitions**: 400ms ease-in-out
- **Loading states**: Continuous, smooth
- **Respect prefers-reduced-motion**: Disable animations if set

### Touch Gestures

- **Swipe left**: Delete item
- **Swipe right**: Complete item / Archive
- **Long press**: Context menu / Additional options
- **Pull to refresh**: Reload data
- **Pinch to zoom**: Calendar month view (optional)

### Empty States

All views should have friendly empty states with:
- Illustrative icon or image
- Clear message explaining what goes here
- Primary action button to add first item
- Optional tips or suggestions

### Loading States

- **Skeleton screens**: For content-heavy pages
- **Spinners**: For quick actions (< 2s)
- **Progress bars**: For multi-step processes
- **Optimistic UI**: Show expected result immediately, rollback if fails
